<div class="sastodealinfo">
<h4>Sastodeal: The One-stop Shopping Destination</h4>
<br/>
<p>About Us</p>
<p>Our story began in Dec 2011, when internet penetration in Nepal was just about 9%. Yet, we were encouraged to start not just a company but an ecommerce industry that would have a significant impact in Nepal’s economy for generations to come. Bootstrapped with just Rs.50,000, we rented a small garage, worked on broken furniture and chairs and worked hard to build a strong company and significantly contributing in building an ecommerce industry. Today,  Sastodeal  is one of the leading ecommerce companies in Nepal with millions of customers and thousands of vendors / partners all over Nepal. We have a logistic network that ensures deliveries in most parts of the nation with exceptions of some locations (work in progress). Our goal is to ensure that our users and customers can buy products at affordable prices, get their products delivered as assured, and on time regardless of their location. On the other hand, we provide a platform for our vendors to cater to millions of customers without additional cost to their business.  
</p>
<p>Sastodeal  Vision</p>
<p>
Our vision is to make Nepal proud by being the best local example in customer experience. </p>

<script>
    (function  () {
        require(['jquery', 'js/popper.min', 'js/bootstrap.bundle.min', 'js/owl.carousel.min','js/voiceSearch'], function ($) {
            $(".menu-dropdown-icon a")
                .click(function(e) {
                    var link = $(this);

                    var item = link.parent("li");
                    
                    if (item.hasClass("active")) {
                        item.removeClass("active").children("a").removeClass("active");
                    } else {
                        item.addClass("active").children("a").addClass("active");
                    }

                    if (item.children(".menu-dropdown-icon").length > 0) {
                        var href = link.attr("href");
                        link.attr("href", "#");
                        setTimeout(function () { 
                            link.attr("href", href);
                        }, 300);
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                })
                .each(function() {
                    var link = $(this);
                    if (link.get(0).href === location.href) {
                        link.addClass("active").parents("li").addClass("active");
                        return false;
                    }
                });
        });
    })();</script>

<script>
    require([
        'jquery',
        'mage/url'
    ], function (
        $,
        murl
    ) {
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(".popup-form-submit").submit(function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();

                
                var emptyCount = 0;
                $('.popup-form-submit input').each(function () {
                    var value = $(this).val();
                    if (value === "") {
                        emptyCount = emptyCount + 1;
                    }
                });

                
                var password = $('.popup-form-submit #password').val();
                var confirmPassword = $('.popup-form-submit #password-confirmation').val();
                $('#submit-sign-up').prop("disabled", false)
                if((emptyCount == 0) && (password === confirmPassword) && ($('.help-text').css('color') === "rgb(0, 128, 0)") &&
                    ($(".popup-form-submit .password .password-weak").length == 0)
                 ) {
                    $.ajax({
                        url: murl.build('customer/account/createpost'),
                        type: "POST",
                        data: $('#customer-form-validate').serialize(),
                        showLoader: true,
                        cache: false,
                        success: function (response) {
                            $('.action-close').trigger('click');
                            $('#product-addtocart-button').trigger( "click" );
                            location.reload();
                            return true;
                        }
                    });
                    return false;
                }
            });
        });
    });</script>

<script>
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {
        $('#email_address').focusout(function () {
            var emailVal = $(this).val();
            var emailValUrl = 'https://www.sastodeal.com/sastomarketplace/account/uniquecustomeremail'
            $('#email_address').siblings('.help-text').remove();
            var mailformat = /^\w+([\.-]?\w+)*@\w+([\.-]?\w+)*(\.\w{2,3})+$/;
            if (!emailVal.match(mailformat)) {
                $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:red;">Email is not valid</span>');
                return false;
            }
            $.ajax({
                showLoader: true,
                url: emailValUrl,
                type: 'POST',
                data: {
                    form_key: $.mage.cookies.get('form_key'),
                    email: emailVal
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                beforeSend: function () {
                    $('body').trigger('processStart');
                },
                success: function (response) {
                    $('body').trigger('processStop');
                    if (response.message) {
                        $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:green;">' + response.message + '</span>')
                        $('#submit-sign-up').prop("disabled", false)
                    }
                },
                error: function (error) {
                    $('body').trigger('processStop');
                    if (error.responseJSON != undefined && error.responseJSON.message) {
                        $('#email_address').after('<span class="help-text" style="color:red;">' + error.responseJSON.message + '</span>');
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });</script>

<script>
    require([
        'jquery'
    ], function ($) {
        let indexCount = 0;
        const maxCount = 10;
        const categorySelector = $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category ol.items li');
        function showMaxCategoryItems() {
            indexCount = 0;
            categorySelector.each(function (element) {
                if(indexCount < maxCount) {
                    $(this).show();
                }
                else {
                    $(this).hide();
                }
                indexCount++;
            });
        }
        showMaxCategoryItems();
        if(indexCount >= maxCount) {
            $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions').show();
        }
        $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-more').click(function (){
            categorySelector.show();
            $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-more').hide();
            $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-less').show();
        });
        $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-less').click(function (){
            showMaxCategoryItems();
            $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-more').show();
            $('#layered-filter-block .filter-options .sd-filter.sd-category .actions .show-less').hide();
        });
    });</script>

<script>
    require([
        'jquery',
        'ibnabmodernizr'
    ], function ($) {
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            $('.menu > ul > li:has( > ul)').addClass('menu-dropdown-icon');
            

            $('.menu > ul > li:has( > ul li)').addClass('megamenu-enabled');
            

            $('.menu > ul > li > ul:not(:has(ul))').addClass('normal-sub');
            

            $(".menu > ul").before("<a href=\"#\" class=\"menu-mobile\">Navigation</a>");

            
            
            
            

            $('.menu > ul > li').hover(function(e) {

                var expanding = $(this);
                
                var timer = window.setTimeout(function () {
                    expanding.data('timerid', null);
                    
                    if ($(window).width() > 943) {
                        expanding.children("ul").stop(true, false).show();
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }

                }, 300);
                
                expanding.data('timerid', timer);
            }, function(e) {

                var timerid = $(this).data('timerid');
                if (timerid != null) {
                    
                    window.clearTimeout(timerid);
                }
                else{
                    $(this).children("ul").hide();
                }
            });

            

            $(".menu > ul > li").click(function () {
                if ($(window).width() <= 943) {
                    $(this).children("ul").fadeToggle(150);
                }
            });
            

            $(".menu-mobile").click(function (e) {
                $(".menu > ul").toggleClass('show-on-mobile');
                e.preventDefault();
            });
        });
    });</script>
